      **************************                                        00010000
       IDENTIFICATION DIVISION.                                         00020000
      **************************                                        00030000
       PROGRAM-ID.    BP13CB0J.                                         00040000
      *AUTHOR.        MARGE LAM KO.                                     00050000
      *DATE-WRITTEN.  26 APR 2017.                                      00060000
                                                                        00070000
      * =========================================================== *   00080000
      * SYSTEM OF COMMITMENT (BP13)                                 *   00090000
      * =========================================================== *   00100000
      *   OBJECTIVE   : THIS PROGRAM RETRIEVES RECORDS FROM         *   00110000
      *                 BP13FD05 AND BP13FD07 TO CREATE RECORDS TO  *   00120000
      *                 GRANT_ASMNT AND GRANT_ASMNT_PERSON          *   00130000
      *                 SO THAT THEY ARE SYNCHRONIZED               *   00140000
      *                 IF THERE IS RECOVERY, WRITE TO GRANT_RCVRY, *   00150000
      *                 EX_GRANT_ASMNT, EX_GRANT_ASMNT_PERSON INSTEAD   00160000
      *                                                             *   00170000
      *   INPUT FILES :                                             *   00180000
      *   1.  BP13FD05                                              *   00190000
      *   2.  BP13FD07                                              *   00200000
      *   3.  BP13K800                                              *   00210000
      *   4.  BP13K820 - TO GET CSTMR SOURCE                        *   00220000
      *   5.  BP13K893 - IF NOT IN K800                             *   00230000
      *   6.  BP13K895 - TO GET CSTMR SOURCE (IF NOT IN K820)       *   00240000
      *                                                             *   00250000
      *   OUTPUT FILE                                               *   00260000
      *   1.  P13FD05A - FD05 NOT FOUND IN FD07                     *   00270000
      *                                                             *   00280000
      *   TABLES:                                                   *   00290000
      *   1.  GRANT_ASMNT                                           *   00300000
      *   2.  GRANT_ASMNT_PERSON                                    *   00310000
      *   3.  GRANT_RCVRY                                           *   00320000
      *   4.  EX_GRANT_ASMNT                                        *   00330000
      *   5.  EX_GRANT_ASMNT_PERSON                                 *   00340000
      *   6.  GRANT_UPDATE_LOG                                      *   00350000
      *                                                             *   00360000
      * CHQ REQ     DATE     BY  DESCRIPTIONS                       *   00370000
      * -------- ---------- ---- ---------------------------------- *   00380000
      * BP13     26/04/2017 MRN1 NEW PROGRAM                        *   00390000
      * BP138971 15/12/2021 KR13 CATER FOR NEW FIN SERIES 'M'       *   00391002
      * =========================================================== *   00400000
                                                                        00410000
       ENVIRONMENT DIVISION.                                            00420000
                                                                        00430000
       CONFIGURATION SECTION.                                           00440000
                                                                        00450000
       SOURCE-COMPUTER. IBM-3090.                                       00460000
       OBJECT-COMPUTER. IBM-3090.                                       00470000
                                                                        00480000
       INPUT-OUTPUT SECTION.                                            00490000
                                                                        00500000
       FILE-CONTROL.                                                    00510000
                                                                        00520000
           SELECT BP13FD07 ASSIGN TO BP13FD07.                          00530000
                                                                        00540000
           SELECT BP13FD05 ASSIGN TO BP13FD05.                          00550000
                                                                        00560000
           SELECT BP13K800 ASSIGN TO BP13K800                           00570000
                  ACCESS MODE     IS DYNAMIC                            00580000
                  ORGANIZATION    IS INDEXED                            00590000
                  RECORD KEY      IS K800-NUM-REGN                      00600000
                  FILE STATUS     IS WS-K800-STATUS.                    00610000
                                                                        00620000
           SELECT BP13K820 ASSIGN TO BP13K820                           00630000
                  ACCESS MODE     IS DYNAMIC                            00640000
                  ORGANIZATION    IS INDEXED                            00650000
                  RECORD KEY      IS K820-KEY-FLD                       00660000
                  FILE STATUS     IS WS-K820-STATUS.                    00670000
                                                                        00680000
           SELECT BP13K893 ASSIGN TO BP13K893                           00690000
                  ACCESS MODE     IS DYNAMIC                            00700000
                  ORGANIZATION    IS INDEXED                            00710000
                  RECORD KEY      IS K893-KEY-FLD                       00720000
                  FILE STATUS     IS WS-K893-STATUS.                    00730000
                                                                        00740000
           SELECT BP13K895 ASSIGN TO BP13K895                           00750000
                  ACCESS MODE     IS DYNAMIC                            00760000
                  ORGANIZATION    IS INDEXED                            00770000
                  RECORD KEY      IS K895-KEY-FLD                       00780000
                  FILE STATUS     IS WS-K895-STATUS.                    00790000
                                                                        00800000
           SELECT P13FD05A ASSIGN       TO P13FD05A.                    00810000
                                                                        00820000
       DATA DIVISION.                                                   00830000
                                                                        00840000
       FILE SECTION.                                                    00850000
                                                                        00860000
       FD   BP13FD07                                                    00870000
            RECORD CONTAINS 700 CHARACTERS                              00880000
            LABEL RECORDS ARE OMITTED                                   00890000
            RECORDING MODE IS F.                                        00900000
       COPY BP13KD07.                                                   00910000
                                                                        00920000
       FD   BP13FD05                                                    00930000
            RECORD CONTAINS 500 CHARACTERS                              00940000
            LABEL RECORDS ARE OMITTED                                   00950000
            RECORDING MODE IS F.                                        00960000
       COPY BP13KD05.                                                   00970000
                                                                        00980000
       FD   BP13K800                                                    00990000
            RECORD CONTAINS 2000 CHARACTERS.                            01000000
       COPY BP13K800.                                                   01010000
                                                                        01020000
       FD   BP13K820                                                    01030000
            RECORD IS VARYING IN SIZE FROM 01 TO 400.                   01040000
      *     RECORD CONTAINS 400 CHARACTERS.                             01050000
       COPY BP13K820.                                                   01060000
                                                                        01070000
       FD   BP13K893                                                    01080000
            RECORD CONTAINS 2050 CHARACTERS.                            01090000
       COPY BP13K893.                                                   01100000
                                                                        01110000
       FD  BP13K895                                                     01120000
           RECORD CONTAINS 450 CHARACTERS.                              01130000
       COPY BP13K895.                                                   01140000
                                                                        01150000
       FD   P13FD05A                                                    01160000
            RECORD CONTAINS 500 CHARACTERS                              01170000
            LABEL RECORDS ARE OMITTED                                   01180000
            RECORDING MODE IS F.                                        01190000
       01  P13FD05A-REC     PIC X(500).                                 01200000
                                                                        01210000
       COPY AV02COMM.                                                   01220000
                                                                        01230000
